					    			onerror="this.onerror='';this.src='/wcsstore/CostcoGLOBALSAS/images/unavailable_350.png';this.alt='No image available';updateViewerIfError();" 
					    			itemprop="image" alt="Sony PlayStation 5 Gaming Console Bundle"/>

	var _LCdiv_ID = "productImageContainer";

<script>
	var zoomViewerJSONObject = {
		xl: 'PZ680',
		lg: 'PZ470',
		md: 'PZ352',
		sm: 'PZ637',
		xs: 'PZ344',
		libraryUrl: 'https://images.costco-static.com/ViewerDelivery/staticService?profileId=12026540&manual_init=true&file=rfxjloader.js&rfx_embed=',
		viewerUrl: 'https://images.costco-static.com/ImageDelivery/imageService?profileId=12026540&itemId=1483712-847&recipeName=',
		videoJqueryUrl: '//d2vxgxvhgubbj8.cloudfront.net' + '/scripts/jquery.liveclicker-latest_c.js',
		videoJsUrl: '//d2vxgxvhgubbj8.cloudfront.net' + '/scripts/client/69/LC_Costco_PDP_1.0.18.js',
		videoCssUrl: '//d2vxgxvhgubbj8.cloudfront.net' + '/scripts/client/69/Costco_PDP_1.0.16.css',

<script type="text/javascript">
	
	/**
	 * NOTE: This code is intended to be invoked as soon as posible, 
	 * which means that webpack will probably not be available so we have to use inline java script.
	 */

	/**
	 * Returns zoom viewer size for the current window width
	 */
	function getViewerSize() {
		var width = $(window).width();
		if (width > 1000 || (width <= 769 && width > 382)) return zoomViewer.xl;
		if (width > 764) return zoomViewer.lg;
		return zoomViewer.xs;
	}
		
	var initZoomViewer = function(modalClosed) {
		
		//adds src attribute to script tag for the Rich Media zoom viewer library
		//and to img tag for the zoom viewer object to initiate injection by Rich Media
		function createViewer(viewerSize) {
			currentViewer = viewerSize;
			downloadLib(viewerSize);
			downloadHero(viewerSize);
		}
		
		function downloadLib(viewerSize) {
			$viewerLib.attr('src', zoomViewer.libraryUrl + viewerSize);
		}
		
		function downloadHero(viewerSize) {
			$viewerImg.attr('src', zoomViewer.viewerUrl + viewerSize.substr(2));
		}
		
		//changes size of viewer if current window size requires a different size
		function updateViewer() {
			var newViewerSize = getViewerSize();		
		
			if (newViewerSize != currentViewer) {
				console.log('PDP: Window resized to new view. Updating zoomViewer. Old view = ' + currentViewer + ', new view = ' + newViewerSize);
				$viewerDiv.css('visibility', 'hidden');
				var element =  document.getElementById('initialProductImage');
				if (typeof(element) != 'undefined' && element != null) {
					element.style.display = '';
				}
				destroyThumbnailCarousel();
				RICHFX.load.fullReset();
				$viewerImg = $('#productImage');
				createViewer(newViewerSize);
				RICHFX.settings.init();
				$('#theViews').removeClass();
			}
			else if ($theViews.children().length) {
				adjustThumbnails();
			}				
			$theViews.find('button').remove();
			adjustSlidesForDesktopView();
			setupTextOverlay();
			bindOpenImageLightboxModal();
			setupTabindexForVideoThumbnail();
		}
		
		//adjusts thumbnail image width and position for desktop view
		function adjustSlidesForDesktopView() {
			
			if (window.innerWidth >= 769) {
				
				$thumbnails.find('img').removeClass('img-fixed-dimensions');
				$thumbnails.find('img').addClass('img-responsive');
				$thumbnails.find('a').not('.slick-active').hide();
			
			} else {
			
				$thumbnails.find('img').removeClass('img-responsive');
				$thumbnails.find('img').addClass('img-fixed-dimensions');
				$thumbnails.find('a').not('.slick-active').show();
			}
		}
		
		//adjusts thumbnail width and position of video overlay images
		function adjustThumbnails() {
			//var thumbWidth = Math.floor($theViews.width() / 6);
			//$theViews.find('a.slick-active:not(:last-child)').css('width', '50px');
			//$theViews.find('a').css('height', '40px');
			var $vidOverlay = $('img[id*=videoOverlay]');
			$vidOverlay.each(function() {
				$(this).parent().css('width', '');
				$(this).parent().css('height', 'auto');
				$(this).css('left', $(this).siblings().position().left);
				$(this).parent().css('display', 'block');
			});
		}
		
		//adds responsive properties to the zoom viewer
		function makeViewerResponsive() {
			var $container = $('.RICHFXViewerContainer');
			$container.css('width', '');
			$container.css('height', '');
			$('#productImageContainer').find('img').addClass('img-responsive');
			$thumbnails.find('img').addClass('img-fixed-dimensions');
		}
		
		//creates thumbnail carousel
		function setupThumbnailCarousel(){
			if (currentSlide == 'undefined') {
				currentSlide = 0;
			}
			if (firstActiveSlide == 'undefined') {
				firstActiveSlide = 0;
			}
			var slides = $theViews.find('a').length;
	
			var responsiveBreakpoints = [];
			for (var i = 0; i < 7; i++) {
				var breakPoint = {
						breakpoint: 370 + (i*50),
						settings: {
							slidesToShow: i + 7,
							slidesToScroll: i + 7
						}
				};
				responsiveBreakpoints.push(breakPoint);
				
			}
			
			var breakPoint = {
				breakpoint: 768,
				settings: {
					slidesToShow: 5,
					slidesToScroll: 5,
					vertical: true
				}
			};
			responsiveBreakpoints.push(breakPoint);
			var carouselOptions = {
			        dots: false,
			        slidesToShow: 5,
			        respondTo: 'slider',
			        infinite: false,
			        slidesToScroll: 6,
			        autoplay: false,
			        draggable: false,
			        accessibility: true,
			        adaptiveHeight: false,
			        mobileFirst: true,
			        responsive: responsiveBreakpoints				
			}
			if($(window).width()<370){
				carouselOptions.slidesToShow = 5;
				carouselOptions.respondTo = 'slider';
			} else if($(window).width()<769) {
				carouselOptions.slidesToShow = 6;
				carouselOptions.respondTo = 'slider';
			} else {
				carouselOptions.slidesToShow = 6;
				carouselOptions.respondTo = 'window';
			}
			COSTCO.util.carousel($theViews,carouselOptions);

			console.log('PDP: Binding keyup event on thumbnails');
			$theViews.find('a').on('keyup', function(e){
				if(e.which==13) //If user use keyboard enter key to select image simulate the click
				{
					console.log('PDP: Thumbnail keyup event triggered, key = ' + e.which);
					if ($(this).find('div.overlay').length == 0) {
						console.log('PDP: Forcing thumbnail click');
						$(this).find('img').click();
					}
					//Move the focus to the selected slide, need to do this as the click simulation reset the focus
					$('.selectedSlide').first().focus();
				}
			});
			adjustThumbnails();
			setupTabindexForVideoThumbnail();	
		}
		//destroys thumbnail carousel
		function destroyThumbnailCarousel() {
			if(!$('#theViews').is(':empty')) {
				$theViews.slick('destroy');
				if($theViews.find('a[tabindex]').length != $theViews.find('a').length ) {
					$theViews.find('a[tabindex]').remove();
				}
			}
		}
		
		//opens image lightbox modal
		function bindOpenImageLightboxModal() {
	
			function openModal(event) {
				console.log('PDP: openModal() called');
				event.stopImmediatePropagation();
				cleanUpEvents();
				COSTCO.ModalImageLightboxView.openImageLightBoxModal(event);
			}
			
			function addADAPropertiesToThumbnails() {
				if($theViews) {
					console.log('PDP: Adding ADA properties to thumbnails');
					$('#theViews').find('a').each(function(index) {
						$(this).find('span').attr('tabindex','-1');
						$(this).attr('tabindex','-1')
						.find('img')
						.attr('tabindex','0')
						.attr('aria-label',messages.PREVIEW + ' ' + (++index));
					});
				}
			}
			
			function bindHeroImageClick() {
				console.log('PDP: Bind hero image click');
				$('#productImageContainer').find('img:visible').each(function(){
					//Cloning the element to clear all events
					$clone = $(this).clone();
					$(this).get(0).parentNode.replaceChild($clone.get(0),$(this).get(0));
					$clone.on('click', function(event){
						console.log('PDP: Hero image clicked');
						openModal(event);
					});
				});
			}
			
			function bindHeroImageEnterKeypress() {
				console.log('PDP: Bind hero image keydown event');
				$('#RICHFXViewerContainer___richfx_id_0').on('keydown', function(event){
					if(event.which==13) {
						console.log('PDP: Hero image keydown event triggered with enter key');
						event.preventDefault();
						openModal(event);
					}
				});
			}
			
			function addTabIndexForHeroImageBD() {
				if('BD'=== $('#applicationType').val() && $('#RICHFXViewerContainer___richfx_id_0').length > 0){
					$('#RICHFXViewerContainer___richfx_id_0').attr('tabindex', 0);
				}
			}
			
			addADAPropertiesToThumbnails();
			bindHeroImageClick();
			bindHeroImageEnterKeypress();
			addTabIndexForHeroImageBD();
		
		}
		
		function cleanUpEvents() {
			document.removeEventListener('richmedia.state.loaded', handleStateLoaded);
			document.removeEventListener('richmedia.swatch.changed', handleSwatchChanged);
			document.removeEventListener('richmedia.view.changed', handleViewChanged);
			$(window).off("resize");
			$('#lcVideo').remove();
		}
		
		//uses liveclicker's scripts to setup videos
		function loadVideoData() {
			console.log('PDP Load: External Video Detected. Loading Liveclicker.');
			$('#liveClickerCss').attr('href', zoomViewer.videoCssUrl);
			$.cachedScript(zoomViewer.videoJqueryUrl).done(function() {
				$.cachedScript(zoomViewer.videoJsUrl);
			});
			document.addEventListener('RichMedia.ExternalVideo.Show', function() {
				$('#zoomInstruction').hide();					
			});
			document.addEventListener('RichMedia.ExternalVideo.Hide', function() {
				$('#zoomInstruction').show();
			});
			
		}
		
		//selects the first available swatch color from our side so
		//that the customer will not see a color that's unavailable.
		function selectInitialSwatch() {
			try {
				COSTCO.CMath.swatchInitialTileSelected = true;
				var swatch = $('.swatchDropdown').find('option[data-swatch]:not([disabled])').first().data('swatch');
				var currentSwatch = $('.swatchDropdown').find('option[data-swatch]:selected').first().data('swatch');
				//Check if currently selected swatch is disabled
				if (currentSwatch != swatch) {
					//trigger a select of the first available swatch color from the color select dropdown
					COSTCO.CMath.triggerSwatchDropDownSelection(swatch);
				}
			}
			catch(e){
			}
			if($('#theSwatches').find('img[alt="'+swatch+'"]').length > 0){
				$('#theSwatches').find('img[alt="'+swatch+'"]').first().click();
			} else {
				var swatchText = $('.swatchDropdown').find('option[data-swatch]:not([disabled])').first().text();
				if($('#theSwatches').find('img[alt="'+swatchText+'"]').first().length > 0) {
					$('#theSwatches').find('img[alt="'+swatchText+'"]').first().click();
				} else {
					//fallback in case swatch is not found by option value or option name
					COSTCO.CMath.triggerSwatchDropDownSelection(swatch);
				}
			}
			$('#product-body-item-number').removeClass('hide');
			$('#product-body-model-number').removeClass('hide');
		}
		
		//out of stock items do not reflect properly in the swatch tiles from rich media
		//so we have to sync their tiles with our product options.
		function syncSwatchTiles(swatchMode) {
			var colorsInStock = $.map($('[data-swatch]', '.swatchDropdown'), function(option) { 
				if($(option).attr("disabled") != "disabled"){
					return $(option).data('swatch').trim().toLowerCase(); 
				}
			});
			var colorsOutStock = $.map($('[data-swatch]', '.swatchDropdown'), function(option) { 
				if($(option).attr("disabled") == "disabled"){
					return $(option).data('swatch').trim().toLowerCase(); 
				}
			});
			var colorsNames = $.map($('[data-swatch]', '.swatchDropdown'), function(option) { 
				if($(option).text().includes(messages.BACKORDER_TEXT)) {
					var sliceStr = ' - '+ messages.BACKORDER_TEXT;
					return $(option).text().slice(0, $(option).text().indexOf(sliceStr))+ " -"+$(option).data('swatch').trim().toLowerCase()+"-";
				} else if($(option).text().includes(messages.OUT_OF_STOCK_TEXT)) {
					var sliceStr = ' - '+ messages.OUT_OF_STOCK_TEXT;
					return $(option).text().slice(0, $(option).text().indexOf(sliceStr))+ " -"+$(option).data('swatch').trim().toLowerCase()+"-";
				} else if($(option).text().includes(' -')) {
					return $(option).text().slice(0, $(option).text().indexOf(' -'))+ " -"+$(option).data('swatch').trim().toLowerCase()+"-";
				} else {
					return $(option).text() + " -"+$(option).data('swatch').trim().toLowerCase()+"-";
				}
			});
			
			$('img', '#theSwatches').each(function() {
				var itemDescriptionArray = $(this).siblings('span.RICHFXColorChangeSwatchName')[0].innerHTML.split(" ");
				if(itemDescriptionArray.length == 2) {
					var color = itemDescriptionArray[1].toLowerCase();
					var colorNameTitle = $.map(colorsNames, function (value){
						if(value.includes(' -'+color+'-')){
							return value.slice(0, value.indexOf(' -'+color+'-')); 
						}
					});
					if (colorsInStock.indexOf(color) < 0 && colorsOutStock.indexOf(color) < 0) {
						$(this).parent().remove();
					} else if(colorsInStock.indexOf(color) < 0 ) {
						$(this).parent().addClass('disabledSwatch');
						if(color == 'white'){
							$(this).parent().append('<img src="/wcsstore/RWDStaticAssets/fonts/fallback-icons/icons/swatch-disabled-grey.png" class="disableOverlaySwatch" />');
						}else {
							$(this).parent().append('<img src="/wcsstore/RWDStaticAssets/fonts/fallback-icons/icons/swatch-disabled-white.png" class="disableOverlaySwatch" />');
						}
						$(this).parent().get(0).setAttribute("tabindex", "-1");
						$(this).parent().wrap('<span class="swatch-help" data-placement="bottom" data-trigger="focus hover" data-toggle="popover" data-html="true" data-content="'+colorNameTitle + ' ' + messages.OUT_OF_STOCK_TOOLTIP + '" />');
						$(this).parent().prepend('<span class="offscreen">' +colorNameTitle + ' '+ messages.OUT_OF_STOCK_TOOLTIP +'</span>');
					}else {
						$(this).parent().get(0).setAttribute("data-sort", colorsInStock.indexOf(color));
						
						$(this).parent().get(0).setAttribute("data-content", colorNameTitle);
						$(this).parent().get(0).setAttribute("data-placement", "bottom");
						$(this).parent().get(0).setAttribute("data-trigger", "focus hover");
						$(this).parent().get(0).setAttribute("data-toggle", "popover");
						$(this).parent().get(0).setAttribute("data-html", "true");
						$(this).parent().get(0).classList.add("swatch-help");
						$(this).parent().get(0).setAttribute("onkeydown", "COSTCO.CMath.runRMAActiveColor(event, '" + color + "')");
						
						if (costcoStoreFeatures.WEBSITE_REDESIGN_V2_PDP_FEATURE_ENABLE) {
							$(this).css('border-radius', '5px');
						}
					}		
				}
			});
			
			
			var sortedSwatches = $('#theSwatches').children().sort(function(a,b){
				return a.getAttribute('data-sort') - b.getAttribute('data-sort');
			});
			
			
			$('#theSwatches').empty();
			$('#theSwatches').append(sortedSwatches);
			if(swatchMode == 2) {
				$('#theSwatches').removeClass('hide');
			}
		}
		
		//Sets up swatches based on swatchMode
		//A loop is introducted to handle if business set the swatch in the second sequence
		//If the swatch is not the first option we do not auto select it 
		//as the first swatch option may not be a valid option given the previous variant selection
		//swatchMode = 1 is the regular dropdown
		//swatchMode = 2 is RichFx's swatch color tiles and we hide our dropdown
		function setupSwatches() {
			let swatchDropdowns = $('.swatchDropdown');
			for(i = 0; i< swatchDropdowns.length; i++) {
				let swatchMode = $(swatchDropdowns[i]).data('swatch-mode');
				if (swatchMode == 1 || swatchMode == 2) {
					syncSwatchTiles(swatchMode);
					if(i == 0)
						selectInitialSwatch();
					//fallback to our select if RichFx's swatch tiles didn't load
					if (swatchMode == 2 && $('#theSwatches').children().length == 0) {
						$('.swatchDropdown').removeClass('hide');
					}
					COSTCO.util.swatch_accesible_popover('.swatch-help');
				} else {
					$('#product-body-item-number').removeClass('hide');
					$('#product-body-model-number').removeClass('hide');
				}
			}
		}
		//setus up the viewer to have responsive properties and
		//shows thumbnails if they are available
		function setupViewer() {
			makeViewerResponsive();
			if ($theViews.find('img').length > 0) {
				$thumbnails.show();
				setupThumbnailCarousel();
			}	
		}
		
		//creates text overlay that displays number of slides not shown
		function setupTextOverlay() {
			
			if ($thumbnails.find('a').length > 0) {
				
				$thumbnails.find('img').removeClass('overlap-img');
				$thumbnails.find('.overlay').remove();
			
				var numberOfHiddenSlides = $thumbnails.find('a').not('.slick-active').length>0 ? $thumbnails.find('a').not('.slick-active').length+1 : $thumbnails.find('a').not('.slick-active').length;
			
				var srAdditionalText = '<span class="sr-only">&nbsp;'+(numberOfHiddenSlides > 1 ? messages.PDP_REDESIGN_V2_MORE_ITEMS_SR_TEXT +'</span>' : messages.PDP_REDESIGN_V2_ONE_ITEM_SR_TEXT +'</span>');
				
				if (numberOfHiddenSlides > 0) {
					var $lastDisplayedSlide = $thumbnails.find('.slick-active').last();
					
					$lastDisplayedSlide.find('img').addClass('overlap-img');
					$lastDisplayedSlide.append('<div class="overlay" tabindex="0">+' + numberOfHiddenSlides + srAdditionalText + '</div>');
					if ($lastDisplayedSlide.width() > 0) {
						$thumbnails.find('.overlay').toggleClass('fixed').width($lastDisplayedSlide.width());
					}							
					if ($lastDisplayedSlide.height() > 10) {
						$thumbnails.find('.overlay').toggleClass('fixed').height($lastDisplayedSlide.height());
					} else {
						$thumbnails.find('.overlay').toggleClass('fixed').height($lastDisplayedSlide.width());
					}
	
					$thumbnails.find('.overlay').on('click', function(event){
						activateOverlay(event);
					});
					$thumbnails.find('.overlay').parent().on('keyup', function(event){
						if(event.which==13) {
							activateOverlay(event); 
						}					
					});
				}
			}
		}
		
		function activateOverlay(event) {
			event.stopImmediatePropagation();
			cleanUpEvents();
			var overlayThumbClicked = true;
			COSTCO.ModalImageLightboxView.openImageLightBoxModal(event, overlayThumbClicked);
		}
		
		//these elements are already available in the DOM so set them
		var $viewerDiv = $('#zoomViewer');
		var $viewerLib = $('#productImageLibrary');
		var $viewerImg = $('#productImage');
		var $realHeroContainer = $('#realHeroContainer');
		var $thumbnails = $('#thumbnails');
		var $theViews = $('#theViews');
		var $initialImage = $('#initialProductImage');
		var viewerSize = getViewerSize();
		var currentViewer = viewerSize;
		var currentSlide = 0;
		var firstActiveSlide = 0;
		
		function setupTabindexForVideoThumbnail() {
		  var $vidOverlay = $('img[id*=videoOverlay]');
		  $vidOverlay.each(function() {
			$(this).attr('tabindex',-1);
		  });
		}

		function handleStateLoaded() {
			//debugger;
			setupViewer();
			setupSwatches();
			//hide the overlayed image after zoom viewer finishes loading
			var element =  document.getElementById('initialProductImage');
			if (typeof(element) != 'undefined' && element != null) {
				element.style.display = 'none';
			}
			$realHeroContainer.removeClass( "hide" )
			$viewerDiv.css('visibility', 'visible');
			var $externalVideo = $theViews.find('img[id*=External]');
			if (typeof lc == 'undefined' && $externalVideo.length > 0) { //only load liveclicker files once
				loadVideoData();
			}
			
			bindOpenImageLightboxModal();
			$theViews.find('button').remove();
			adjustSlidesForDesktopView();		
			setMainImage();	
			refocusElement();
			setupTextOverlay();
			setupTabindexForVideoThumbnail();
			makeHeroImageADACompliant();
		}
		
		function setMainImage() {
    		let currentSlide = $('#theViews').find('a')[0];
    		if(currentSlide){
				var $theViews = $('#theViews');
				if($theViews) {
					$theViews.find('img').each(function(){
						$(this).off("click");
					});
				}
        		$(currentSlide).find('span').next().click(); 			
    		}
		}
		
		function handleViewChanged() {
			console.log('PDP: handleViewChanged() called');
			if(!$('body').hasClass('image-lightbox-modal-open')){
				var $selected = $('.RICHFXColorChangeViewSelected');
				destroyThumbnailCarousel();
				setupThumbnailCarousel();
				bindOpenImageLightboxModal();
				$theViews.find('button').remove();
				adjustSlidesForDesktopView();
				setupTextOverlay();
				currentSlide = $selected.parent().index();
				setTimeout(function(){
					var currentImageIndex = $selected.closest('a').index();
					if (currentImageIndex == 0) {
						currentImageIndex = 1;
					} else {
						if (!hasVideo($theViews)) {
							currentImageIndex = currentImageIndex + 1;
						}
					}
					$('div[id ^="RICHFXViewerContainer___richfx_id_"][tabindex=0]').find('img').removeAttr("aria-label");
					$('div[id ^="RICHFXViewerContainer___richfx_id_"][tabindex=0]').find('img').removeAttr("title");
					$('div[id ^="RICHFXViewerContainer___richfx_id_"][tabindex=0]').find('img').attr("alt","");
					$('img[id ^="RICHFXViewerContainer___richfx_id_"][id $="_initialImage"]').attr("alt", messages.PDETAIL_VIEW_LARGER_IMAGE + " " + currentImageIndex);
					focusHeroImage();
				}, 500);
			}	
		}
		
		function handleSwatchChanged() {
			if ($theViews.hasClass('slick-initialized')) {			
				destroyThumbnailCarousel();
				currentSlide = 0;
				firstActiveSlide = 0;
				setupThumbnailCarousel();
				bindOpenImageLightboxModal();
				$theViews.find('button').remove();
				adjustSlidesForDesktopView();
				setupTextOverlay();
			}
		}
		
		// Focus element that had focus before image Lightbox opened.
		function refocusElement() {
			var $elementToFocus = $("#"+$('#lastFocusedElement').val()).parent();
			if ($elementToFocus.length) {
				$elementToFocus.focus();
				$('#lastFocusedElement').remove();		
			}
		}
				
		
	  	//when richmedia is done loading their stuff, we have to make some adjustments
		if(modalClosed) {
			cleanUpEvents();
			document.addEventListener('richmedia.view.changed', handleViewChanged);		
			document.addEventListener('richmedia.swatch.changed', handleSwatchChanged);
			var $externalVideo = $theViews.find('img[id*=External]');
			if ($externalVideo.length > 0) {
				loadVideoData();
			}			
		} else {
			document.addEventListener('richmedia.state.loaded', handleStateLoaded);
			document.addEventListener('richmedia.view.changed', handleViewChanged);		
			document.addEventListener('richmedia.swatch.changed', handleSwatchChanged);
		}
		
		function resizeViewer() {
		  //modify viewer size on window resize
		  $(window).resize(COSTCO.util.debounce(updateViewer, 250));
		}

		if (typeof COSTCO !== 'undefined') {
		  resizeViewer();
		} else {
		  document.addEventListener("CostcoGlobalLoaded", resizeViewer, false);
		}
	}
	
	// Set initial swatch values on page load and image lightbox close
	function setInitialSwatchValues() {
		let hasOptions = $("select[type=select-variants]");
		if (hasOptions.length > 0) {
			$("select[type=select-variants]").each(function(){
				$(this).find('option[data-swatch]:not([disabled])').first().prop("selected", "selected");
				COSTCO.CMath.update_selected_option_label($(this).find('option:selected').val());
			});
			$('.swatches-v2').each(function(){
				$(this).find('input').prop('checked', false);
				$(this).find('input:enabled').first().prop('checked', true);
			});
			// Change the quantity of all bundle variances to 0 at load
			$('input[id^="quantity-"]').each(function(){
				$(this).val('0');
				$(this).trigger('change');
			});
		}
	}

	//Makes hero image focusable - function is called only on inital load
	function makeHeroImageADACompliant() {
		setTimeout(function(){
			$('#RICHFXViewerContainer___richfx_id_0_initialImage').removeAttr("aria-label");
			$('#RICHFXViewerContainer___richfx_id_0_initialImage').removeAttr("title");
			$('#RICHFXViewerContainer___richfx_id_0_initialImage').attr("alt", messages.PDETAIL_VIEW_LARGER_IMAGE + " 1");
		}, 1000);
		
	}

	// Sets focus on image that is hero at the moment
	function focusHeroImage() {
		$("#RICHFXViewerContainer___richfx_id_0").focus();
	}
	function hasVideo(views) {
		var $externalVideo = views.find('img[id*=External]');
		if ($externalVideo.length > 0) {
			return true;
		}
		return false;
	}

	$(window).load(function() {
		setInitialSwatchValues();
	});
		

	/**
	 * Self invoking fn that will be invoked immediately after hero image placeholder ( <img id="productImage" ) is rendered in HTML. It does following:
	 * 1. Loads hero image
	 * 2. On hero image loaded event:
	 *	2.1 Register richmedia event listeners
	 *	2.2 Download richfx lib
	 */
	(function() {
		console.log('PDP Load: Setting richfx hero image src - START');
		var viewerSize = getViewerSize();
		var heroImage = zoomViewer.viewerUrl + viewerSize.substr(2);
		console.log('PDP Load: Hero image src: ' + heroImage);
		var heroLoaded = false;
		var $viewerImg = $('#productImage');
		$viewerImg.on('load', function () {
			if (heroLoaded === false) {
				console.log('PDP Load: Enter hero image load');
				heroLoaded = true;
				
				initZoomViewer();

				var richfxLibSrc = zoomViewer.libraryUrl + viewerSize;
				console.log('PDP Load: Richfx JS lib src: ' + richfxLibSrc);
				
				var $viewerLib = $('#productImageLibrary');
				$viewerLib.on('load', function() {
					console.log('PDP Load: Richfx JS lib downloaded');
					
					/**
					 * Checks if manual_init=true is set in the richfx JS lib url
					 */
					function isManualInitEnabled(libSrc) {
						return /manual_init=true/.test(libSrc);
					}
					
					if (isManualInitEnabled(richfxLibSrc)) {
						console.log('PDP Load: manual_init set to true. Manually invoking RICHFX.init()');
						RICHFX.init();
					} else {
						console.log('PDP Load: manual_init not set. Let richfx invoke the init()');
					}
				});
				
				$viewerLib.attr('src', richfxLibSrc);
				console.log('PDP Load: Exit hero image load');
			} else {
				console.log('PDP Load: Hero already loaded');
			}

		});
		
		/*
		 *  This is required for safari browser, safari will not trigger regular 'load' event if image is served from cache (ususally second open of modal)
		 */
		if ($viewerImg[0].complete) { 
			console.log('PDP Load: Manually triggered event for image loaded');
			$viewerImg.load();
		}

		$viewerImg.attr('src', heroImage);
		console.log('PDP Load: Setting richfx hero image src - END');
		
	})();
</script>

<div data-bi-placement="Criteo_Product_Display_Page_Espot"  id="viewItem-Carousel"></div><!-- Display the actual text ENDS here --><!-- End - CostcoGLOBALSAS\Snippets\Marketing\ESpot\RenderRwdESpotContent.jspf --><!-- DEBUG SearchProvider:  Order of Catentry IDs from CMC: [] --><!-- END ContentAreaRwdESpot.jsp Criteo_Product_Display_Page_Espot -->

	<script>
		function getCriteoUniversalParams() {
            var uParams ={
                scriptSrc : '//dynamic.criteo.com/js/ld/ld.js?a=48266',
                uat : 'false',
                account : '48266',
                retailerVisitorId : COSTCO.COT.getRetailerVisitorId(),
    			email : COSTCO.COT.getEmail(),
            }
            return uParams;
	    }

		function loadCriteo() {
			var eventSpecificParams = {
				event : 'viewItem',
				pageId : COSTCO.util.isMobile() ? 'viewItem_M' : 'viewItem',
				item: '100691489',
				price: 'NjM5Ljk5',
				availability: '0',
			};
			COSTCO.COT.fireEvent($.extend(eventSpecificParams, getCriteoUniversalParams()));
		};

		function loadCriteoAddToCartParams(partNumber, price, quantity){
			var eventSpecificParams = {
				event : 'addToCart',
				itemId: partNumber,
				price: price,
				quantity: quantity,
				zipCode : '',
				storeId : '10301',
			}
			COSTCO.COT.fireEvent($.extend(eventSpecificParams, getCriteoUniversalParams()));
		};

		$('body').bind('costco.cart.item.added', function (event, data) {
			loadCriteoAddToCartParams(data.partNumber, data.price, data.quantity);
	    })

		try{
			if(typeof COSTCO != "undefined" && COSTCO && typeof COSTCO.COT != "undefined" && COSTCO.COT && typeof COSTCO.util != "undefined" && COSTCO.util){
				loadCriteo();
			}else {
				document.addEventListener("CostcoSubModulesLoaded", loadCriteo, false);
			}
		
		}catch(e){
		
			if(costcoloadstate.submodules){				
				loadCriteo();
			}else {
				document.addEventListener("CostcoSubModulesLoaded", loadCriteo, false);
			}
		}
	</script>

				psku: '1483712',

				categories: '[Electronics, Video Games & Consoles, PlayStation]',
				storeid: 'US'
			}, {wcapiVersion: '2.0'});
		})();

		function addToCartWindsorParams(partNumber, price, quantity, inventory, url){
			analytics.track('Added Product', {
				id: '100691489',
				vsku: '100691489',
				psku: partNumber,
				name: 'Sony PlayStation 5 Gaming Console Bundle',
				price: price,
				available: inventory,
				cartLink: url,
				quantity: quantity,
				storeid: 'US'
			}, {wcapiVersion: '2.0'});
		};
		
		$('body').bind('windsor.product.cart.item.added', function (event, data) {
			var cartPageUrl = window.location.origin + '/CheckoutCartDisplayView';
			addToCartWindsorParams(data.partNumber, data.price, data.quantity, data.inventory, cartPageUrl);
		});

	</script>

	getDataUrl : "/AjaxMembershipMetaDataView?langId=-1&storeId=10301&catalogId=10701",
	payload : "",
	resultCode: "",
	funktions : new Array(),
	getDrawFunctions: function(){
		var widgets = $("div[data-membership-widget-draw-function]");
		for (var i = 0; i < widgets.length; ++i) {
			var funktion = $(widgets[i]).data('membership-widget-draw-function');	
    		MembershipMetaData.funktions.push(funktion);
    		
		}
	},
	processAjaxReturn:	function(data){
		COSTCO.util.LoginTimeout.updateActivity();
		
		// if resultCode is a failure message code, then payLoadData will not be fetched
		// which shall show an error message staying in edit mode of widget
		
		if(data != undefined){
		
			MembershipMetaData.payload = data;
			for (var i = 0; i < MembershipMetaData.funktions.length; ++i) {
  				var namespaces = MembershipMetaData.funktions[i].split(".");
  				var func = namespaces.pop();

				var regExp = /\(([^)]+)\)/; //get stuff from ()
				var matches = regExp.exec(func);
				if(matches==null){
					window[namespaces][func]();
				}
				else {
					var func1 = func.slice(0, func.indexOf("("));
					var param1 = matches[1]!=null?matches[1]:"";
					param1 = param1.replace(/\"/g, "").replace(/\'/g, "");

	  				try {
	 					window[namespaces][func1](param1);
	  				} catch(err){
					  console.log("Error in Calling Draw Widget" +namespaces+ ": " +err);
					}
				}
			}
			
			if (MembershipMetaData.payload.errorMessages.length > 0){
				for (var i = 0; i < MembershipMetaData.payload.errorMessages.length; ++i) {
					$('#crmMetaDataGlobalError').html(MembershipMetaData.payload.errorMessages[i]);
				}
				$('#crmMetaDataGlobalError').show();
				$('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: $('#crmMetaDataGlobalError') });
			}else{
				$('#crmMetaDataGlobalError').hide();
			}
			if(data.caller.usageRole != '01'){
				$('#digitalConnection').remove();
				$('#mailConnection').remove();
			}
			COSTCO.util.updateCappJson();
			COSTCO.util.processCappLogic();
		}
	},
	ajaxHandler : function(url, payload){
		
		COSTCO.util.LoginTimeout.checkTimeout();
		
		var pseudo = (new Date()).getTime();
		$.ajax({
			type: 'POST',
			url: url+"&pseudo="+pseudo,
			dataType: 'json',
			data: payload,
			success: function(data) { 
				COSTCO.util.LoginTimeout.updateActivity();
				MembershipMetaData.processAjaxReturn(data);
				$(".r1_spinnerFirstLoad").hide();
			},
			timeout: wcs.ajaxTimeout,
			error: function(x, t, m) {
				COSTCO.util.LoginTimeout.updateActivity();
        		if(t==="timeout") {
        			
        		} else {
		    	    
        		}
    		}
		});
	},
	getHumanReadablePrefix : function(prefixCode){
		if (prefixCode == "0001"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["0001"]
		}else if (prefixCode == "0002"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["0002"]
		}else if (prefixCode == "0003"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["0003"]
		}else if (prefixCode == "0004"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["0004"]
		}else if (prefixCode == "Z005"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["Z005"]
		}else if (prefixCode == "Z001"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["Z001"]
		}
		return prefixCode;
	},
	getHumanReadableSuffix : function(suffixCode){
		if (suffixCode == "0001"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0001"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0002"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0002"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0003"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0003"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0004"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0004"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0005"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0005"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0006"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0006"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0007"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0007"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "Z001"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["Z001"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "Z002"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["Z002"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "Z003"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["Z003"]
		}
		return suffixCode;
	},
	unProtectFields : function(jqSelector){
		var formFields = $(jqSelector).find("input[type='text']  ,select");
		
		for (var i = 0; i < formFields.length; ++i) {
			var protect = $(formFields[i]).data("membership-widget-protect-field");
			
			if (MembershipMetaData.FIELD_TYPE.READ_ONLY != protect){
				if( $(formFields[i]).is('input')){
					$(formFields[i]).attr('readonly', false);
					$(formFields[i]).css({border: "1px solid #dbdbdb"});
				}else{
					$(formFields[i]).attr('disabled', false);
				}
				if(MembershipMetaData.FIELD_TYPE.EDITABLE_REQUIRED == protect){
					//$(formFields[i]).rules('add', { required:true});
					
				}else if (MembershipMetaData.FIELD_TYPE.DO_NOT_DISPLAY == protect){
					$(formFields[i]).val('');
					if( $(formFields[i]).is('input')){
						$(formFields[i]).attr('readonly', true);
						$(formFields[i]).css({border: "none"});
					}else{
						$(formFields[i]).attr('disabled', true);			
					}
				}	
			}
		}
	},
	protectFields : function(jqSelector){
		var formFields = $(jqSelector).find("input[type='text']  ,select");
		for (var i = 0; i < formFields.length; ++i) {
			if( $(formFields[i]).is('input')){
				$(formFields[i]).attr('readonly', true);
				$(formFields[i]).css({border: "none"});
			}else{
				$(formFields[i]).attr('disabled', true);			
			}
		}
	},
	protectDisplayFields : function(jqSelector){
		for (var i = 0; i < jqSelector.length; ++i) {
			var protection = $(jqSelector[i]).data('membership-widget-protect-field');	
    		if (MembershipMetaData.FIELD_TYPE.DO_NOT_DISPLAY == protection){
    			$(jqSelector[i]).hide();
    		}else{
    			$(jqSelector[i]).show();
    		}
		}
	},
	ajaxSend : function(){
		var spinner = '<div class="ui-widget-overlay ui-front r1_spinner" id="crmMetaDataGlobalSpinner"></div>'
		$("body").append( spinner );
	},
	ajaxComplete : function(){
		$('#crmMetaDataGlobalSpinner').remove();
	}
}

// Changing document.ready to window.onload, document.ready not workingin some pages for some reason
$(window).load(function(){
	
			if(typeof skipFooterMembershipMetaDataCall == 'undefined' || skipFooterMembershipMetaDataCall == false){
				var mosInfo = COSTCO.util.getMemberCookie();
				MembershipMetaData.getDataUrl = "https://" + location.hostname + "/AjaxCitiMembershipMetaDataView?langId=-1&storeId=10301&catalogId=10701";
				if($.cookie("capp_json") == null && mosInfo && mosInfo.signedIn == true && mosInfo.costcoMember == true){
					MembershipMetaData.ajaxHandler(MembershipMetaData.getDataUrl, null);
				}
			}
		
});

<script>
  //select only promo fields if a visible price is displayed - no static pages or prices hidden by due to MAP
  $(document).ready(function() {
    var promoRegex = /^\$+(\d|,\d|(\.\d{2}))+\s+((-+\s+\$+(\d|,\d|(\.\d{2}))+\s+OFF)|OFF)+((?!.)|(\s+&+))/i;
    $("div.caption:has(div.price:visible) p.promo").each(function() {
      var promoText = $(this).text().trim();
      if (promoRegex.test(promoText)) {
        $(this).text("After " + promoText);
      }
    });
    setTimeout(function() {
      $("div.caption:has(h3.price:visible) p.promo").each(function() {
        var promoText = $(this).text().trim();
        if (promoRegex.test(promoText)) {
          $(this).text("After " + promoText);
        }
      });
    }, 2000);
  });
</script>
